    genre_id INT,
    PRIMARY KEY (song_id, genre_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (song_id) REFERENCES songs(song_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (genre_id) REFERENCES genres(genre_id)
);

    PRIMARY KEY (song_id, genre_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (song_id) REFERENCES songs(song_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (genre_id) REFERENCES genres(genre_id)
);
